In [2]:
# Accessing the account through developer tokens
import tweepy

consumer_key = 'HIDDEN'
consumer_secret = 'HIDDEN'
access_token = 'HIDDEN'
access_secret = 'HIDDEN'

auth = tweepy.OAuthHandler(consumer_key, consumer_secret)
auth.set_access_token(access_token, access_secret)

api = tweepy.API(auth)
In [3]:
# Rmoving the Time limiter.
api = tweepy.API(auth_handler=auth, wait_on_rate_limit=True, wait_on_rate_limit_notify=True)
In [4]:
# Reading the twitter archive for accessing the tweets Id
df1 = pd.read_csv('twitter-archive-enhanced.csv')
In [5]:
# Grabbing all the tweet Ids into single expression
tweet_ids = df1['tweet_id'].values
In [39]:
# Writing a loop to write all the values for tweet ids into json.txt file
count = 0
fails_dict = {}
start = timer()

with open('tweet_json.txt', 'w') as outfile:
    
    for tweet_id in tweet_ids:
        count += 1
        print(str(count) + ": " + str(tweet_id))
        try:
            tweet = api.get_status(tweet_id, tweet_mode='extended')
            print("Success")
            json.dump(tweet._json, outfile)
            outfile.write('\n')
        except tweepy.TweepError as e:
            print("Fail")
            fails_dict[tweet_id] = e
            pass
end = timer()
print(end - start)
print(fails_dict)

In [40]:
# Appending all the information extracted from json.text into a Dataframe
tweet_api = pd.DataFrame(columns = ['tweet_id','favorite_count','retweet_count'])
with open ('tweet_json.txt') as file:
    for line in file:
        status = json.loads(line)
        tweet_id = status['id']
        favorite_count = status['favorite_count']
        retweet_count = status['retweet_count']
        tweet_api = tweet_api.append(pd.DataFrame([[tweet_id,favorite_count,retweet_count]],
                                                 columns = ['tweet_id','favorite_count','retweet_count']))
tweet_api = tweet_api.reset_index(drop = True)
tweet_api

440 rows × 17 columns

Assessment For Quality ( for twitter archive )¶

  1. Various ratings where denominator is not 10.
  2. Various Null values for columns in_reply_to_status_id in_reply_to_user_id retweeted_status_id retweeted_status_user_id
  3. Incorrect Data type for tweet Id
  4. Renaming Columns with more appropriate name
  5. The names are not all correct.
  6. The Denominator can't be zero
  7. Removal of all the Retweets
  8. Non-Inclusion of Float numerators

Assessment ForTidiness ( for twitter archive )¶

  1. Various stages of dogs is de-classified
  2. Timestamp Column needs to be seperated with Time and Date
  3. The clarity In source of text must be shown.

2. Coding¶

DEFINE (A)¶

Remove all the retweets from text sections by using str.contains()

CODE (A)¶
In [15]:
twitter_archive_enhanced = twitter_archive_enhanced[twitter_archive_enhanced["text"].str.contains("RT")==False]
TEST (A)¶
In [16]:
twitter_archive_enhanced[twitter_archive_enhanced["text"].str.contains("RT")==True]
Out[16]:

DEFINE (B)¶

Extract Ratings from the text as correct ratings and split them on the basis of delimeter (' \ ') and make new columns from the both splitted values.

CODE (B)¶
In [17]:
# Extract ratimg from text
twitter_archive_enhanced['ratings'] = twitter_archive_enhanced.text.str.extract('([0-9]*\d\/\d\d)', expand=True)

DEFINE (C)¶

As per we rate doges guidelines, they rate dog on the base of 10, so there is no chance that any values could be else than 10. We will turn all the non 10 values to 10

CODE(C)¶
In [20]:
twitter_archive_enhanced.loc[(twitter_archive_enhanced.rating_denominator != 10 ),'rating_denominator']=10

In [21]:

DEFINE (E)¶

After assessing the data without program I've found that some of the names were incorrect. So I will extract all the names from the text section and create a new series for it.

CODE (E)¶
In [24]:
#Extracting dog_name from the text column
text_dog_name = []
for text in twitter_archive_enhanced.text:
  name_search = re.search('([Tt]his is\s\w+)', text) or re.search('([Mm]eet\s\w+)', text)
  if name_search:
    # split the string and choosing last word
    name = name_search.group().split()[-1]
    text_dog_name.append(name)
    
text_dog_name

DEFINE (F)¶

As we know that the doggo, floofer, pupper and puppo are the four stages of the dogs. But somehow they are all differently categorised in the different columns so we need to extract them all into single column named stage.

CODE (F)¶
In [27]:
# Replacing the Null Values with space for proper concatanation
twitter_archive_enhanced['doggo'] = twitter_archive_enhanced['doggo'].replace('None','',regex = False)
twitter_archive_enhanced['floofer'] = twitter_archive_enhanced['floofer'].replace('None','',regex = False)
twitter_archive_enhanced['pupper'] = twitter_archive_enhanced['pupper'].replace('None','',regex = False)
twitter_archive_enhanced['puppo'] = twitter_archive_enhanced['puppo'].replace('None','',regex = False)
In [28]:
# Adding all the values together
twitter_archive_enhanced['stage'] = twitter_archive_enhanced['doggo']  + twitter_archive_enhanced['floofer']  + twitter_archive_enhanced['pupper'] + twitter_archive_enhanced['puppo']
In [29]:
#Handling multiple stages in dog_stage column
twitter_archive_enhanced.loc[twitter_archive_enhanced.stage=='doggopupper', 'dog_stage'] = 'doggo , pupper'
twitter_archive_enhanced.loc[twitter_archive_enhanced.stage=='doggopuppo', 'dog_stage'] = 'doggo , puppo'
twitter_archive_enhanced.loc[twitter_archive_enhanced.stage=='doggofloofer', 'dog_stage'] = 'doggo , floofer'
In [30]:
twitter_archive_enhanced.loc[twitter_archive_enhanced.stage=='', 'stage'] = np.nan
In [31]:
# Dropping all the Unnecessary Columns
twitter_archive_enhanced.drop(['in_reply_to_status_id','in_reply_to_user_id','retweeted_status_id','retweeted_status_user_id','retweeted_status_timestamp','expanded_urls','doggo','floofer','pupper','puppo','rating_numerator','rating_denominator','name'],axis = 1 , inplace = True)

DEFINE (G)¶

Timestamp columns is readable but with a bit of difficulty. So it will be a good idea to extract time and date from the Timestamp column and make them both as seperate column.

CODE (G)¶
In [33]:
# Splitting the Date and time from Timestamp
twitter_archive_enhanced['Date'] = twitter_archive_enhanced['timestamp'].str[:10]
twitter_archive_enhanced['Time'] = twitter_archive_enhanced['timestamp'].str[10:]
In [34]:
# Stripping Time Zones from Time
twitter_archive_enhanced['Time'] = twitter_archive_enhanced['Time'].str[:-6]
# Dropping the timestamp table
twitter_archive_enhanced.drop(['timestamp','ratings'],axis = 1, inplace = True)

DEFINE (H)¶

The source from which the tweets were made were some links. Readability was bit difficult. So I will replace all the the source values with some easy and readable values.

CODE (H)¶
In [36]:
# Replacing the source values with readable forms
twitter_archive_enhanced['source'] = twitter_archive_enhanced['source'].str.replace('<a href="http://twitter.com/download/iphone" rel="nofollow">Twitter for iPhone</a>','iPhone')
twitter_archive_enhanced['source'] = twitter_archive_enhanced['source'].str.replace('<a href="http://vine.co" rel="nofollow">Vine - Make a Scene</a>','Vine')
twitter_archive_enhanced['source'] = twitter_archive_enhanced['source'].str.replace('<a href="http://twitter.com" rel="nofollow">Twitter Web Client</a>','Twitter_Web_Client')
twitter_archive_enhanced['source'] = twitter_archive_enhanced['source'].str.replace('<a href="https://about.twitter.com/products/tweetdeck" rel="nofollow">TweetDeck</a','Tweet_Deck')
In [37]:
# Fixing the error
twitter_archive_enhanced['source'] = twitter_archive_enhanced['source'].str.replace('Tweet_Deck>','Tweet_Deck')

Assessment For Quality ( for image predcitions )¶

DEFINE (J)¶

Uneven Cases of Letters in p1,p2 and p3 & Replacement of '_' with ' ' & Removal of Uneven Spaces

CODE (J)¶
In [48]:
# Converting all the names for p1,p2,p3 into lower case
image_predictions['p1'] = image_predictions['p1'].str.lower()
image_predictions['p2'] = image_predictions['p2'].str.lower()
image_predictions['p3'] = image_predictions['p3'].str.lower()
In [49]:
# Replacing "_" with ' '
image_predictions['p1'] = image_predictions['p1'].str.replace('_',' ')
image_predictions['p2'] = image_predictions['p2'].str.replace('_',' ')
image_predictions['p3'] = image_predictions['p3'].str.replace('_',' ')

DEFINE (K)¶

DEFINE (N)¶

Now as we cleaned almost all the data. Now it is time to merge all the datasets into one. We will change datatypes and columns names ahead.

CODE (N)¶
In [60]:
# Merge fucntion to merge twitter_archive and image_predictions
master_df_pt1 = pd.merge(twitter_archive_enhanced, image_predictions, on='tweet_id', how='left')
In [61]:
# Converting variables into respective datatypes
tweets['tweet_id']=tweets['tweet_id'].astype(np.int64)
master_df_pt1['tweet_id']=master_df_pt1['tweet_id'].astype(np.int64)

tweets['tweet_id']=tweets['tweet_id'].astype(int)
master_df_pt1['tweet_id']=master_df_pt1['tweet_id'].astype(int)
In [62]:
# merge command to merge previously merged df to tweets
master_df = pd.merge(master_df_pt1, tweets,on=['tweet_id'],how='left')
In [63]:

  1. Pupper is the most popular dog stage
  2. Standard poodle is the dog with most retweets.
  3. Eskimo dog of doggo stage is the dog with most retweets.
  4. Golden retriever is the dog with the most popularity
